- **Commerce product workflow webhook update**: `POST /api/admin/sites/:siteId/commerce/products/:productId/provider-sync` and `POST /api/admin/sites/:siteId/commerce/products/:productId/subscriptions/:orderId/action` now dispatch `site-updated` webhooks after successful provider catalog sync and product-scoped subscription lifecycle actions in both demo and repository modes. Payloads include compact product/order before/after summaries, provider status, execution mode, subscription action metadata, request id, actor, `content`/`collections`/`commerce` changed-key metadata, and route-specific source markers so storefront builds, product automation, subscription status panels, cache workers, and external commerce integrations can react to Backy-owned provider workflow mutations without scraping order/product records.
- **Commerce order workflow webhook update**: `POST /api/admin/sites/:siteId/commerce/orders/:orderId/quote`, `/tracking`, and `/fulfillment` now dispatch `site-updated` webhooks after successful quote refreshes, tracking refreshes, and fulfillment dispatches in both demo and repository modes. Payloads include compact order before/after summaries, quote totals/provider adjustment status, tracking status/provider metadata, fulfillment dispatch metadata, request id, actor, `content`/`collections`/`commerce` changed-key metadata, and route-specific source markers so custom admin frontends, storefront cache workers, order-status integrations, and provider automation listeners can react to order execution workflow changes.
- **Commerce order label/refund webhook update**: `POST|DELETE /api/admin/sites/:siteId/commerce/orders/:orderId/shipping-label` and `POST|PATCH /api/admin/sites/:siteId/commerce/orders/:orderId/provider-refund` now dispatch `site-updated` webhooks after successful label preparation, label voiding, provider refund requests, and provider refund refreshes in both demo and repository modes. Payloads include compact order before/after summaries, label or refund status/provider/amount metadata, request id, actor, `content`/`collections`/`commerce` changed-key metadata, and route-specific source markers so storefront cache workers, order-status views, fulfillment automation, and refund integrations can react to label/refund execution changes without scraping collection records.
- **Commerce/orders action contract update**: the shipping-label read/create/void API, fulfillment dispatch/read API, tracking refresh/read API, and provider-refund read/create/refresh API now return private/no-store Backy contract headers for `backy.shipping-label.v1`, `backy.fulfillment-dispatch.v1`, `backy.tracking.v1`, and `backy.provider-refund.v1`, matching the quote and analytics endpoints so custom admin clients can rely on consistent schema/cache metadata across order execution actions.
- **SDK commerce admin operations bridge**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes typed authenticated methods for the remaining commerce admin handoff routes: order quote read/refresh, tracking read/refresh, provider-refund read/create/refresh, fulfillment read/dispatch, shipping-label read/create/void, site reconciliation dry-runs, product provider-sync, and product subscription lifecycle read/action calls. Generated type fixtures and SDK smoke coverage exercise the read/dry-run paths without exposing provider secrets or mutating live provider accounts, making the `/products` and `/orders` custom-admin API bridge closer to the Wix/WordPress-style external frontend goal while live provider certification remains Partial.
- **Commerce/orders reconciliation contract update**: site reconciliation, platform batch reconciliation, and cron-readiness APIs now expose private/no-store Backy contract headers with `backy.commerce-reconciliation.v1`, `backy.commerce-reconciliation-batch.v1`, and `backy.commerce-reconciliation-readiness.v1`, closing the remaining order-operations response metadata gap for scheduled/manual repair workflows.
- **Commerce/orders webhook contract update**: commerce provider webhook settlement now returns private/no-store Backy contract headers for `backy.commerce-webhook.v1` on success, duplicate, and error paths so provider integrations and custom dashboards can rely on the same response metadata as the rest of the order execution surface.
- **Commerce/orders handoff contract update**: `/orders` now renders an Order API response contracts panel and includes an `apiContracts` block in the exported handoff manifest, mapping analytics, quote, shipping-label, fulfillment, tracking, provider-refund, webhook settlement, site reconciliation, platform reconciliation, and cron-readiness endpoints to their `backy.*.v1` schema versions, private cache scope, supported methods, and response headers for custom admin frontends.
- **Commerce/orders smoke stability update**: `/orders` now honors `orderId` deep links even when the target order is not present in the first paginated order batch, fetching the record directly and prepending it to the workspace state. The route also refreshes the selected deep-linked order when the URL search state changes, which keeps provider-refund refresh cards visible after smoke/API mutations update the record outside the initial list load. `apps/admin/scripts/orders-smoke.mjs` now deep-links to the mutated order before asserting the provider-refund refresh action, and `npm run ci:commerce-provider-smoke` passes end-to-end for commerce plus orders provider mock coverage, including the previously failing provider-refund refresh path.
- **Template registry admin contract update**: `GET /api/admin/sites/:siteId/templates` now exposes a normalized `backy.template-registry.v1` admin registry backed by persisted `site.settings.frontendDesign.templates`. The response groups page, blog post, form, product, collection, and reusable-section templates by type, includes content summaries, binding hint counts, canvas metadata, and returns exact `frontendDesignTemplateId` clone payloads for the existing page/blog/form/reusable-section/collection/product create APIs. `test:frontend-contract` source-guards the route, helper, clone targets, and API docs so admin surfaces and custom frontend builders can discover the template registry without parsing the full frontend-design contract. `test:template-registry` behavior-tests registry grouping, filtering, summaries, and clone payloads for page, form, and product templates.
- **Template registry admin UI update**: `/sites/:siteId` now surfaces a Template registry summary inside the Frontend design contract panel, including the registry endpoint, `backy.template-registry.v1` schema, `frontendDesignTemplateId` clone field, clone target count, and supported page/blog/form/product/collection/section template types. `test:site-detail` checks that the operator-facing panel renders the registry summary beside capture/save controls, while typechecks keep the admin response contract aligned with the public API response.
- **Template registry operator list update**: the same `/sites/:siteId` Frontend design contract panel now lists captured templates from the current design contract with type labels, clone endpoints, and route patterns, so operators can inspect page/blog/form/product/collection/section template availability without editing raw JSON. `test:site-detail` verifies the list after saving a custom frontend-design contract, including visible page/blog template names and clone-target URL text.
- **Template registry workspace action update**: captured templates listed on `/sites/:siteId` now include operator actions that deep-link page and blog templates into `/pages/new` and `/blog/new` with the selected `frontendDesignTemplateId`, matching the `backy.template-registry.v1` clone field, while form, product, collection, and section templates route to their existing site-scoped template workspaces with a `frontendTemplate` search id that highlights the selected captured template on arrival. `test:site-detail` checks all six captured page/blog/form/product/collection/section template types and their operator actions beside the saved custom frontend-design contract so the registry is not only informational.
- **Template registry deep-link guard update**: `test:frontend-contract` now source-guards that `/sites/:siteId` passes `frontendTemplate` into form/product/collection/section workspaces, that those workspaces validate and highlight the selected captured template, and that the collection draft route preserves the selected frontend template when `draft=new` resets the schema form.
- **Template registry runtime smoke update**: `test:frontend-design` now verifies unauthenticated `/api/admin/sites/:siteId/templates` access is rejected, the frontend-design response advertises `endpoints.templates` plus the `backy.template-registry.v1` summary, and authenticated registry reads return grouped page/form/product clone payloads, field/element summaries, clone targets, and filtered `type=product&search=product` results after a six-template frontend-design contract is patched.
- **SDK frontend-design/template admin bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes `adminFrontendDesign()`, `updateAdminFrontendDesign()`, `importAdminFrontendDesign()`, `captureAdminSiteDefaults()`, `captureAdminContentTemplate()`, and `adminTemplates()` for custom builder shells. The helpers use the same admin-session/API-key/bearer auth options as live-management, type the normalized `backy.template-registry.v1` registry, preserve `frontendDesignTemplateId` clone bodies for page/blog/form/product/collection/section creation, and are covered by SDK generated-type checks plus smoke read assertions.

- **Editor history shortcut metadata update**: undo and redo toolbar controls now expose stable action ids plus shortcut metadata for Cmd/Ctrl+Z, Cmd/Ctrl+Y, and Shift+Cmd/Ctrl+Z. `apps/admin/scripts/editor-drag-smoke.mjs` source-guards the history command affordances alongside the existing keyboard handler.

- **Editor shell panel shortcut update**: the shared canvas editor now exposes stable shell actions and shortcut metadata for Components (B), Inspector (I), Layers (L), and Focus (F). - **Editor grouping shortcut accessibility update**: the editor group and ungroup toolbar plus inspector controls now expose stable action ids and `aria-keyshortcuts` for Cmd/Ctrl+G and Shift+Cmd/Ctrl+G, including the single selected-group ungroup action. `apps/admin/scripts/editor-drag-smoke.mjs` can run a source-only guard for the grouping shortcut accessibility contract.
- **Editor nested child-selection update**: the shared page/post/section canvas editor now exposes a direct child-layer selection command for selected containers and groups. Authors can use the toolbar button, inspector button, or Shift+Cmd/Ctrl+A to select all visible unlocked direct children before grouping, alignment, duplication, delete, or layer-order commands, and `apps/admin/scripts/editor-drag-smoke.mjs` source-guards the toolbar, inspector, and shortcut contract.
- **Editor sibling-scope selection update**: select-all-siblings now exposes Cmd/Ctrl+A shortcut metadata in the toolbar and is available from both single and multi-layer inspector cards. This keeps same-parent selection setup local to the properties workflow before grouping, alignment, duplicate, delete, and layer-order operations.
- **Editor distribution control labelling update**: multi-selection inspector distribution controls now expose explicit horizontal and vertical labels, and the editor source guard covers toolbar plus inspector distribution controls so spacing operations remain discoverable during nested component layout work.
- **Editor multi-group ungroup update**: the shared canvas editor now treats ungroup as a true multi-selection command when every selected layer is an unlocked editor group in the same parent scope. Shift+Cmd/Ctrl+G, the toolbar, and the inspector can expand all selected groups in one history-tracked operation, preserve child geometry/responsive metadata, and select the expanded children for the next alignment, grouping, duplicate, or delete action.
- **Editor common-parent selection update**: multi-selected child layers in the same nested scope now keep a parent-selection command in the inspector and through the existing Shift+Enter shortcut path. Single-selection inspector parent, child, and child-scope controls now expose shortcut metadata for Shift+Enter, Enter, and Shift+Cmd/Ctrl+A, keeping child-scope selection, grouping, ungrouping, alignment, duplicate, and delete workflows navigable in complex page components.
- **Editor multi-selection action update**: selected-layer clipboard and destructive actions now derive enabled states from the active sibling scope rather than just the primary selection, label single versus multi-layer actions in the toolbar, and expose copy, duplicate, cut, paste, and delete controls in the multi-selection inspector. This keeps nested child selections and grouped component selections actionable without forcing authors back to the top toolbar.
- **Editor paste-target and shortcut metadata update**: the shared canvas editor now exposes shortcut metadata for copy, cut, paste, duplicate, and delete controls in the toolbar and multi-selection inspector. Paste also publishes whether it will insert into the selected unlocked container/group or onto the canvas root via stable `data-paste-target` and target-id metadata, keeping nested component authoring behavior inspectable for smoke coverage and custom editor clients.
- **Editor single-selection inspector action update**: the selected-layer inspector now exposes copy, duplicate, cut, paste, and delete actions for a single selected layer, including shortcut metadata and the same paste-target attributes used by the toolbar. This makes common layer operations available while authors stay in the properties panel for nested component editing.
- **Editor deterministic clone-id update**: duplicate and copy/paste now remap root and nested element ids from the source id using collision-safe `-copy` suffixes instead of timestamp/random ids. The focused clipboard smoke verifies deterministic paste, redo, and duplicate selection ids, and the source guard blocks the clone helper from returning to `generateId()`.
- **Editor inspector visibility/lock update**: single and multi-layer inspector cards now expose hide/show and lock/unlock controls backed by the same selected-layer handlers as the toolbar. The controls preserve selected-layer labels, disabled states, and pressed state metadata so layer state changes remain local to the properties workflow during nested component editing.
- **Editor inspector layer-order update**: toolbar arrange controls now expose bracket shortcut metadata, and single plus multi-layer inspector cards expose local send-to-back, send-backward, bring-forward, and bring-to-front controls backed by the same `handleZOrderChange` path. This keeps layer stacking changes available while authors work in the properties panel.
- **Editor dataset action-plan update**: the Data panel now renders and exports selected-element `backy.editor.dataset-binding-action-plan.v1` and repeater `backy.editor.repeater-dataset-action-plan.v1` contracts. Authors can see collection, field, target, preview, query handoff, slot coverage, records URL, layout, and join-strategy readiness before publishing or handing a collection-bound section to a custom frontend.
- **Editor composition handoff update**: the shared canvas editor inspector now renders `backy.editor-composition-readiness.v1` metrics for total layers, groups, nested child layers, breakpoint overrides, and current selection scope, plus a copyable `backy.editor-composition-action-plan.v1` so grouped page/post/section component trees can be handed to custom admin or frontend builders without reverse-engineering the editor UI.
- **Media ownership coverage reconciliation**: the stale platform-gap Media note no longer treats per-site ownership enforcement as missing. The media admin route tree under `/api/admin/sites/:siteId/media` imports `requireAdminAccess` across list/upload, asset detail, signed URLs, folders, bind/unbind, transforms, retained versions, and provider analytics, with `media.view`, `media.create`, `media.edit`, `media.delete`, and `media.configure` gates applied by route type. `apps/admin/scripts/media-smoke.mjs` covers denied `media.edit` and `media.configure` workflows plus source-guards labelled delete confirmation dialogs, confirm/cancel action labels, visible focus rings for destructive asset, bulk asset, and folder actions, and the copyable media attribution handoff contract, while `apps/public/scripts/admin-site-scope-smoke.mjs` denies non-member access to nested media list/create/provider-analytics routes with `FORBIDDEN_SITE_SCOPE`. Remaining Media risk is external cloud provider-account automation, not ownership scoping or custom-frontend attribution handoff.
- **Blog authoring gap-summary reconciliation**: the stale top-level gap prose no longer lists categories, tags, authors, featured images, scheduling, revisions, or feeds as missing Blog primitives. Those are covered by the verified Blog list/create/editor routes and their admin/public APIs; the remaining Blog risk is now documented as canonical editor/content contract convergence and visual QA rather than absent editorial workflow controls.
- **Public delivery gap-summary reconciliation**: the stale public-delivery note no longer treats custom-domain discovery, CORS, domain metadata, or locale route variants as missing primitives. `GET /api/sites?identifier=` resolves published sites by id, slug, or custom domain in demo and repository modes; `GET /api/sites/:siteId/manifest` exposes managed/custom/verification domains, canonical bases, locale strategy, locale route variants, sitemap/robots URLs, and SDK database-certification metadata; `apps/public/src/proxy.ts` applies configured-origin CORS headers. Remaining public-delivery risk is hosted custom-domain/edge certification, with future feed additions required to stay inside the public envelope/cache contract.
- **Settings custom-frontend CORS handoff update**: `/settings` now includes `BACKY_CORS_ALLOWED_ORIGINS` in the deployment env contract, release-certification handoff manifest, and visible runbook copy so operators can configure exact browser origins for custom frontends without storing those origins as Backy settings. `GET /api/admin/settings` also returns non-secret `runtimePublicApi` evidence for normalized exact origins, origin count, wildcard denial, and exposed Backy contract headers, so the Settings env contract can show server-side CORS readiness. `apps/admin/scripts/settings-smoke.mjs` and `apps/public/scripts/settings-admin-contract-smoke.mjs` source-guard the public API env profile, CORS env key, runtime summary, and release runbook text while public CORS execution remains enforced by `apps/public/src/proxy.ts`.
- **Preview-token actor-binding update**: page and blog preview-token creation now binds the token record and tokenless `previewToken.create` audit metadata to the resolved admin session actor or service-key actor instead of trusting caller-provided actor headers. The admin contract smoke asserts page and post preview audits keep redacting the raw token while carrying concrete actor-binding metadata. Remaining preview risk is usage-audit hardening for public preview reads, not unaudited creation.
- **Preview-token usage audit update**: successful page, blog, render, resolve, and hosted HTML preview-token reads now record tokenless `previewToken.use` audit events with `actorId: "public-preview"`, target type/id, surface, path/slug metadata, and `tokenStored: false` in demo and repository modes. The admin contract smoke exercises tokenized page and post public API, render, and resolve reads after creating preview tokens, reads back the matching use-audit entries, and verifies the raw token is not stored in use metadata. Remaining public-delivery risk is hosted custom-domain/edge certification, with future public feed additions required to keep the same contract/cache headers.
- **Hosted feed error-contract update**: hosted sitemap, robots, and RSS route 404s for missing or unpublished sites now return through `publicContractResponse` with `x-backy-contract-version`, `x-backy-request-id`, `x-backy-cache-scope: error`, and `no-store` caching instead of bare text responses. `apps/public/scripts/admin-contract-smoke.mjs` guards the three hosted route sources against reintroducing bare `new NextResponse('Not found')` feed errors.
- **Frontend comments discovery update**: `GET /api/sites/:siteId/manifest` now exposes a structured `backy.comments-discovery.v1` comments module with resolved comment policy, public approved-list status, moderation statuses, report reasons, report/blocklist endpoint templates, and spam-protection field names. `frontend-manifest.schema.json`, generated SDK contract types, `BackyManifestCommentsModule`, `frontend-contract-smoke`, and SDK smoke source now guard the shape so generated/custom frontends can build discussion and moderation UI without hardcoding Backy comment route details.
- **SDK comment input builder update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exports `buildBackyCommentInput()` for generated/custom page and blog comment forms. The helper normalizes content aliases, author identity aliases, reply/thread ids, guest/user identity, honeypot, started-at, captcha-token, moderation-mode, request-id, and rate-limit metadata into the canonical payload accepted by `submitPageComment()` and `submitBlogComment()`. SDK generated-type checks, SDK smoke assertions, API docs, and the SDK README guard the helper while the Frontend manifest/OpenAPI/SDK APIs row remains Partial for the disposable Supabase/Postgres SDK smoke gate.

The helper normalizes reason/category aliases, reporter identity aliases, details/message/note aliases, and request ids into the canonical `reportComment()` payload. The public report route now returns the normalized report object promised by OpenAPI and records report details in `comment-reported` event metadata for custom moderation dashboards. SDK generated-type checks, SDK smoke assertions, API docs, and the SDK README guard the helper while the Frontend manifest/OpenAPI/SDK APIs row remains Partial for the disposable Supabase/Postgres SDK smoke gate.

The evidence covers database/Supabase, storage/media delivery, Vercel deployment/secrets, notification delivery, commerce provider bridge, public API/CORS, interactive component sandbox, and release certification readiness, names the `BACKY_SETTINGS_PROVIDER_CERTIFICATION_REQUIRED=1 npm run ci:settings-provider-certification` gate, reports covered/missing scenario counts, and keeps database URLs, provider credentials, service-role keys, Vercel tokens, notification secrets, and commerce secrets private. `apps/admin/scripts/settings-smoke.mjs` source/runtime guards the panel so the remaining `/settings` and Settings admin API Partial rows stay tied to credentialed provider execution evidence rather than a broad checklist.
- **Settings launch-readiness handoff update**: `/settings` now renders a command-center `settings-launch-readiness` panel with copyable `backy.settings-launch-readiness.v1` JSON and a `backy.settings-launch-action-plan.v1` action plan. The handoff summarizes delivery mode, public/admin API contract counts, media storage, database/Supabase, CORS contract headers, security, notification, commerce, interactive runtime, and the exact release/database/provider gates without exporting provider secret values. `apps/admin/scripts/settings-smoke.mjs` source-guards the schema, copy action, action plan, no-secret boundary, and rendered command-center layout while the Settings rows remain Partial until credentialed provider and disposable database certification gates pass.
- **Commerce provider certification gate wording update**: the operator-facing `/products` and `/orders` completion gate is `npm run ci:commerce-provider-certification` or the manual Commerce Provider Certification workflow with explicitly selected payment, tax, shipping, discount, catalog, subscription, and webhook provider families. That CI path runs `test:commerce-provider-certification-preflight-contract`, the non-secret release certification doctor, a safe local or external target summary, and then the live provider readiness checks, while repeatable mock coverage remains `npm run ci:commerce-provider-smoke`. The Products/Orders Partial rows therefore stay tied to real provider-family execution and selected credential/input readiness, not mock coverage alone. `npm run test:commerce-provider-certification-preflight-contract` source-guards this audit wording.
- **Public commerce provider env template update**: public manifest `data.modules.commerce.providerCertification`, commerce catalog, commerce order contract, site-scoped OpenAPI, generated SDK types, and the convenience SDK commerce contract now expose `operatorEnvTemplate` for `.env.backy-commerce-provider-certification` using `backy.commerce-provider-certification-env-template.v1`. The template mirrors the guarded Commerce provider command with the release doctor, all `BACKY_COMMERCE_CERTIFY_*` selectors, and `BACKY_COMMERCE_PROVIDER_CERTIFICATION_REQUIRED=1` while keeping real provider credentials in CI/local shell variables, so custom storefronts can display the same live-provider setup handoff that `/products` and `/orders` expose in admin.
- **Public commerce provider manifest schema update**: `specs/ai-frontend-contract/frontend-manifest.schema.json` now treats `data.modules.commerce.providerCertification` as a required first-class custom storefront contract instead of an untyped additional property. Generated SDK contract types export `GeneratedBackyFrontendManifestCommerceProviderCertification`, require `providerCertification` on the commerce manifest module, and type the command template, `.env.backy-commerce-provider-certification` handoff, runtime readiness booleans, provider-family choices, and evidence groups so third-party storefronts cannot lose live-provider setup guidance while still passing manifest type checks.
- **SDK commerce order input builder update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exports `buildBackyCommerceOrderInput()` for generated/custom storefront checkouts. The helper accepts the commerce runtime alias contract advertised by manifest/OpenAPI (`items`, `lineItems`, `cartItems`, `cart.items`, product slug/id aliases, `qty`, top-level customer aliases, payment objects, coupon codes, and checkout-session objects), then emits the canonical private-order payload with normalized email, discount code, checkout session id, and quantity bounds before `createCommerceOrder()`. SDK generated-type checks, SDK smoke assertions, API docs, and the SDK README guard the helper while `/products` and `/orders` remain Partial for credentialed live-provider certification.
- **SDK commerce admin handoff methods update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes `commerceOrderAnalytics()`, `commerceProductProviderSync(productId)`, and `syncCommerceProductProvider(productId, { provider })` for authenticated custom admin clients. These methods use the same per-call admin auth options as Settings/live-management, read private/no-store order analytics, inspect product catalog-sync state, execute the audited product provider-sync route, and return bounded provider-certification evidence without exposing provider credentials or raw private order payloads. SDK generated-type checks, SDK smoke read assertions, API docs, and the SDK README guard the helpers while `/products` and `/orders` remain Partial for credentialed live-provider certification.
- **SDK commerce platform reconciliation bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes `commerceReconciliationReadiness()` and `scheduledPlatformCommerceReconciliation({ dryRun, limit, siteId })` for external operations dashboards. The helpers wrap the existing private `/api/admin/commerce/reconcile/readiness` and `/api/admin/commerce/reconcile` contracts, returning cron-readiness evidence, platform batch reconciliation summaries, per-site skipped/error results, and private/no-store schema metadata without importing the admin UI or exposing provider secrets. SDK generated-type checks, SDK smoke assertions, API docs, and the README guard the bridge while `/products` and `/orders` remain Partial for credentialed live-provider certification.
- **SDK commerce record admin bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes first-class product and order CRUD helpers for external commerce dashboards: `adminCommerceProducts()`, `createAdminCommerceProduct()`, `adminCommerceProduct()`, `updateAdminCommerceProduct()`, `deleteAdminCommerceProduct()`, `adminCommerceOrders()`, `createAdminCommerceOrder()`, `adminCommerceOrder()`, `updateAdminCommerceOrder()`, and `deleteAdminCommerceOrder()`. The helpers default to Backy's audited `products` and private `orders` collection-record APIs, support `collectionId` overrides for custom commerce schemas, and keep the existing collection validation, RBAC, audit, webhook, cache-invalidation, and dynamic-content behavior instead of adding a parallel commerce record store. SDK generated-type fixtures, read-only smoke assertions, API docs, and the README guard the bridge while `/products` and `/orders` remain Partial for credentialed live-provider certification.
- **SDK CMS/commerce batch record bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes the existing audited collection-record CSV export, CSV import, and bulk delete/status-update workflows through `adminCollectionRecordsCsv()`, `importAdminCollectionRecordsCsv()`, and `bulkAdminCollectionRecords()`, plus commerce aliases `adminCommerceProductsCsv()`, `importAdminCommerceProductsCsv()`, `bulkAdminCommerceProducts()`, `adminCommerceOrdersCsv()`, `importAdminCommerceOrdersCsv()`, and `bulkAdminCommerceOrders()`. These helpers keep product/order and generic CMS batch operations on the same RBAC, validation, audit, webhook, import-error, cache-invalidation, and collection schema paths used by the admin UI, giving external WordPress-like admin consoles real batch management without importing `apps/admin`.
- **SDK CMS backup portability bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes `exportAdminCollectionsBackup()` and `importAdminCollectionsBackup()` for custom CMS migration, staging, and multi-site cloning tools. The helpers wrap the audited `backy.collections.backup.v1` JSON export/import routes, preserve schema-plus-record payloads, support selected collection ids, record inclusion toggles, upsert imports, request ids, and admin auth options, and return typed import counts plus cache-invalidation metadata so external WordPress-like admin consoles can move collection schemas and data without scraping `/collections`.
- **SDK Forms admin handoff methods update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes typed custom-admin access for Forms CRUD, Forms analytics, contact segments, saved contact lists, submission moderation, and contact status operations through `adminForms()`, `createAdminForm()`, `adminForm()`, `updateAdminForm()`, `deleteAdminForm()`, `formsAnalytics()`, `formContactSegments()`, `formContactLists()`, `saveFormContactList()`, `deleteFormContactList()`, and per-call admin auth options on the existing submission/contact methods. SDK generated-type checks, SDK smoke read assertions, API docs, and the SDK README guard the methods while `/forms` remains Partial for the configured Supabase/Postgres certification run.
- **SDK Forms action-button bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes the remaining Forms page action workflows for external form builders and CRM consoles: `cloneAdminForm()`, `createAdminFormEmbedBlock()`, `reviewFormSubmission()`, `retryFormSubmissionWebhook()`, `retryFormSubmissionEmail()`, `applyAdminFormConsentRetention()`, and `applyAdminFormsConsentRetention()`. The documented `POST /api/admin/sites/:siteId/forms/:formId/submissions/:submissionId/review` route now delegates to the same audited review implementation as the existing PATCH route, keeping moderation, contact-share, collection-write, audit, and request-id behavior aligned across admin UI and SDK callers while `/forms` remains Partial for the external Supabase/Postgres gate.
- **SDK Forms contact/CRM bridge update**: `packages/sdk-js` now exposes the remaining contact automation workflows behind the Forms and Contacts admin surfaces: `createFormContact()`, `importFormContactsCsv()`, `promoteFormContactToUser()`, `promoteFormContactToCustomer()`, `syncFormContacts()`, and `applyFormContactConsentRetention()`. The helpers wrap Backy's existing validation, billing-seat checks, invite creation, private customer collection promotion, selected-contact webhook sync, CSV row errors, and contact consent retention routes with the same per-call admin auth options, so external CRM consoles can manage leads without importing the admin app while `/forms` remains Partial for the external Supabase/Postgres gate.
- **Products launch-readiness handoff update**: `/products` now renders a selected-product `products-launch-readiness` panel with a copyable `backy.product-launch-readiness.v1` JSON handoff. The checklist scores storefront API readiness, product identity, publish state, pricing, stock/variants, media, checkout/order-intake, delivery/fulfillment, SEO/merchandising, and provider catalog sync, then includes blocker/attention next steps inside the product handoff manifest at `providerExecution.selectedProductLaunchReadiness`. `apps/admin/scripts/commerce-smoke.mjs` source-guards the schema, copy action, action plan, and rendered Products layout so product launches cannot silently lose the sellability handoff while the row remains Partial for live provider certification.

- **Orders provider certification evidence update**: `/orders` now renders `orders-provider-certification-evidence` inside the live provider certification panel, includes non-secret `backy.order-provider-certification-evidence.v1` scenario coverage in the exported provider handoff, and mirrors the same scenario-evidence handoff from `GET /api/admin/sites/:siteId/commerce/orders/analytics` for custom admin clients. - **Orders status-handoff update**: `/orders` now renders a selected-order `orders-status-handoff` panel with a copyable `backy.order-status-handoff.v1` JSON handoff for custom storefront order-confirmation pages, customer portals, and support widgets. The handoff keeps raw orders private while exposing a bounded customer-safe projection with masked contact data, payment state, fulfillment/tracking state, refund state, private-queue safety checks, and the selected order operation action plan. `apps/admin/scripts/orders-smoke.mjs` source-guards the schema, copy action, action-plan bridge, and rendered Orders layout so customer order-status projections cannot silently drift while the row remains Partial for live provider certification.

## Current conclusion

Backy now has most primary admin/editor/API surfaces in the Ready column, with the current table audit at **39 Ready / 6 Partial / 0 Prototype / 0 Missing**. The next milestone is to keep closing one Partial surface at a time, prioritizing durable repository-backed persistence, live Supabase/Postgres smoke coverage, full RBAC/workspace scoping, generated frontend contracts, and provider execution paths before adding unrelated visual controls.
